<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
    var url = new URL(window.location); // Construct URL object using current browser URL
    var params = url.searchParams; // Get query parameters object
    var S4Kcentre = params.get("S4Kcentre"); // Get value of S4Kcentre
    $("#S4Kcentre").val(S4Kcentre); // Set it as the dropdown value
    $("select").change(function(){
        $(this).find("option:selected").each(function(){
            var optionValue = $(this).attr("value");
            window.history.pushState(null, null, "?S4Kcentre=" + optionValue);
            if(optionValue){
                $(".centre").not("." + optionValue).hide();
                $("." + optionValue).show();
            }
        });
    }).change();
});
